GT: c0*epsilon**c1 + c2*(T - c3)*sin(epsilon)
Candidate formulas: 77

I need to determine if any candidate formula can match the GT: `5.889184448896621*epsilon**3 + 2.8821771197066277*(T - 279.6235977851866)*sin(epsilon)`

This expands to: `5.889*epsilon**3 + 2.882*T*sin(epsilon) - 806.08*sin(epsilon)`

The GT has three essential terms:
1. `epsilon**3` (a cubic term in epsilon, no T dependence)
2. `T*sin(epsilon)` (T times sin(epsilon))
3. `sin(epsilon)` (a constant times sin(epsilon))

Let me check candidates that could produce `epsilon**3` and `T*sin(epsilon)` terms.

**Candidate 24**: `T*c0*epsilon**c1 + c2*epsilon**c1 + c3 + c4*epsilon + c5*sin(c6*epsilon + c7)`

Setting c1=3: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + c2*epsilon**3 + c3 + c4*epsilon + c5*sin(c6*epsilon + c7)`

This gives `(T*c0 + c2)*epsilon**3 + c3 + c4*epsilon + c5*sin(c6*epsilon + c7)`. We need `sin(c6*epsilon + c7)` to equal `sin(epsilon)`, so c6=1, c7=0. Then we need c3=0, c4=0. This gives: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + c2*epsilon**3 + c5*sin(epsilon)`.

But GT has `T*sin(epsilon)` - a term where T multiplies sin(epsilon). In candidate 24, T only multiplies `epsilon**3`. So this can't work.

**Candidate 41**: `T*c0*epsilon**c1 + c2*epsilon**c1 + c3 + c4*sin(c5 + c6*epsilon)`

Same issue - T only multiplies epsilon**c1, not sin.

**Candidate 68**: `T*c0*sin(c1*epsilon + c2) + c3 + c4*exp(c5*epsilon)*cos(c6*epsilon)`

This has `T*sin(...)` but needs `epsilon**3` from `exp(c5*epsilon)*cos(c6*epsilon)`, which can't produce a polynomial.

**Candidate 53**: `T*c0*epsilon + T*c1 + c2 + c3*sin(c4*epsilon + c5)` - No epsilon**3 term possible.

**Candidate 72**: `T*c0*epsilon + c1 + c2*sin(c3*epsilon + c4) + c5*epsilon` - No epsilon**3 or T*sin.

**Candidate 2**: `T*c0*epsilon**c1 + c2 + c3*epsilon**c1 + c4*epsilon + c5*exp(c6*epsilon)*sin(c7*epsilon + c8)`

Setting c1=3, c6=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + c2 + c3*epsilon**3 + c4*epsilon + c5*sin(c7*epsilon + c8)`. Same issue - T doesn't multiply sin.

Now I need a candidate where T multiplies a sin term AND has epsilon**3.

**Candidate 68**: `T*c0*sin(c1*epsilon + c2) + c3 + c4*exp(c5*epsilon)*cos(c6*epsilon)` - can't get epsilon**3.

**Candidate 39**: `c0 + c1*sin(c2*epsilon + c3) + c4*epsilon**c5*exp(T*c6)` - This has `exp(T*c6)`, not `T*sin(epsilon)`.

**Candidate 75**: `c0 + c1*exp(c2*epsilon)*cos(c3*epsilon) + c4*epsilon*(T + c5)**c6`

Setting c6=1: `c4*epsilon*(T + c5)` = `c4*T*epsilon + c4*c5*epsilon`. But we need T*sin(epsilon), not T*epsilon.

After careful review, none of the candidates have the structure that produces both `epsilon**3` (or equivalent polynomial) AND `T*sin(epsilon)` simultaneously. The GT requires T to multiply sin(epsilon) and a pure epsilon**3 term. Most candidates either have T multiplying a power of epsilon (not sin) or have exponential/trig terms without T coupling to sin.

No candidate can reproduce the GT structure.
